# 主线关联：导航宗族的秘密

[返回同伴目录](../README.md) | [返回卡西娅目录](README.md) | [下一章](02_形同陌路.md)

导航宗族的秘密

Secrets of the Navis Nobilite

### 任务简介

导航宗族的星站对任何信息都没有反应，但俄歇矩阵探测到了星站舱室内的生物特征。行商浪人唯一的选择就是紧急登陆舰站，亲自调查那里发生了什么事情。

The Navis Nobilite station is not responding to any signals, but the augur arrays have detected biological signatures in the main chamber. The Rogue Trader's only option is to perform an emergency docking and personally investigate.

### 区域

科罗努斯扩区

Koronus Expanse

### 目标

#### 1. 探寻星站，寻找答案

##### 标题

探寻星站，寻找答案

Explore the station to find answers

##### 描述

行商浪人需要招募一名新的导航者，但导航宗族没有任何回应。他们的星站发生了某些古怪的事情，似乎需要外来人员进行干预。

The Rogue Trader needs to recruit a new Navigator, but the Navis Nobilite heralds are not responding, and something strange is happening on their void station. It appears outside intervention is required.

##### 目的地

欧拉克五号星站

Eurac V

#### 2. 重新启动电梯

##### 标题

重新启动电梯

Restart the elevator

##### 描述

根据星站的守护者所言，这里发生了暴乱，一群疯子抓走了他的女主人。目前，卡西娅女士被囚禁在了上层大厅，但电梯发生了故障，任何人都无法前往该区域。

The Keeper of the Station spoke of a rebellion and madmen who captured his mistress. Lady Cassia is being held in the upper chambers against her will, but a malfunctioning elevator prevents anyone from entering.

##### 附加条目

- 附加 1
  - 中文: 行商浪人需要使用守卫室的沉思者来恢复电梯的电力。
  - English: The power to the elevator must be restored using the cogitator in the guard room.

- 附加 2
  - 中文: 控制手杖可以在实验室通过血液与神圣机械重制。
  - English: The elevator control rod can be rebuilt in the laboratory using blood and a sacred mechanism.

#### 3. 回到费雷克处

##### 标题

回到费雷克处

Return to Felek

##### 描述

行商浪人重新制作了控制手杖，恢复了基地的电力供应。是时候前往星站守护者处，前往导航者女士所在的房间了。

The Rogue Trader has recreated the control rod and restored power to the elevator. It is time to return to the Keeper of the Station and ascend to the lady's chambers.

#### 4. 把那个怪物带到费雷克身边

##### 标题

把那个怪物带到费雷克身边

Bring the monster to Felek

##### 描述

事实证明，卡西娅女士并非陷入困境的无辜少女，而是多年来一直恐吓、威胁奥赛罗家族的恶毒怪物。她的能力可以让家族的导航者发疯，只要一个眼神就能夺走他们的生命。费雷克恳求行商浪人答应他最后一个请求：前往上层大厅，用发光的护身符削弱那个怪物的力量，把她带回到费雷克身边，让她接受审判。

It turns out that Lady Cassia is no damsel in distress but a vicious monster who has been terrorising House Orsellio for years. She is capable of driving a Navigator insane and killing them with a single glance. The Keeper has asked the Rogue Trader to grant him one last request: to ascend to the upper chambers, weaken the beast with a glowing charm, and bring her back to Felek for judgement.

#### 5. 拯救导航者女士

##### 标题

拯救导航者女士

Save the lady

##### 描述

叛乱分子得到了神秘的武器。这种武器蕴含导航者的力量，如果星站的守护者打算与叛军正面冲突，恐怕会被叛军的武器立刻杀害。费费雷克恳求行商浪人答应他最后一个请求：前往女主人的房间，将护身符带给她，并将那群叛徒绳之以法。在这之后，行商浪人需要把卡西娅女士带到下层房间的守卫身边。

The rebels have acquired mysterious weapons imbued with the powers of Navigators. The Keeper of the Station will immediately perish if he tries to fight them. Felek has asked the Rogue Trader to grant him one last request: to ascend to the mistress's chambers, give her the charm, and bring the traitors to justice. After that, Lady Cassia must be returned to her people on the lower level.

#### 6. 与星站的女主人交谈

##### 标题

与星站的女主人交谈

Talk to the mistress of the station

##### 描述

费雷克·奥赛罗死在了行商浪人手上。现在，行商浪人必须前往上层大厅，与卡西娅女士交谈，弄清费雷克所说的一切是否属实。

Felek Orsellio has died at the hand of the Rogue Trader. Only speaking with Lady Cassia in the upper chambers will show if he was telling the truth about his mistress.

#### 7. 收集有关导航者的信息

##### 标题

收集有关导航者的信息

Find information on the Navigators

##### 描述

这座星站的守护者，导航者费雷克·奥赛罗已经死了，但行商浪人依然还有希望。欧拉克五号星站还有其他存活的导航者，或许他们愿意加入行商浪人的队伍。

Felek Orsellio, Navigator and Keeper of the Station, is dead. Hope remains that there are some other warp guides left on Eurac V who are ready to join the Rogue Trader.

##### 附加条目

- 附加 1
  - 中文: 每座舰站都会记载所有居民的详细信息，这些信息可能会揭露导航者的所在位置。
  - English: Every station is required to store details about its inhabitants. It may contain information on the Navigators' whereabouts.

- 附加 2
  - 中文: 电梯的电力已经恢复，控制手杖的两个部分都在行商浪人手上。是时候启动电梯，前往上层大厅了。
  - English: Power has been restored to the elevator, and the Rogue Trader has both parts of the control rod. It is time to start the lift and ascend to the upper chambers.

#### 8. 重新启动电梯

##### 标题

重新启动电梯

Restart the elevator

##### 描述

整个星站依然存活的导航者都处于上层大厅区域。行商浪人需要恢复电梯的电力，使用控制手杖前往上层大厅。

The only surviving Navigators on the station can be found in the upper chambers. It is necessary to restore the power to the lift and use a control rod to reach them.

##### 附加条目

- 附加 1
  - 中文: 行商浪人可以通过守卫室的沉思者来恢复电梯的电力。
  - English: The power to the elevator can be restored using the cogitator in the guard room.

- 附加 2
  - 中文: 得到了控制手杖的两个部分之后，就可以控制电梯了。沉思者的数据显示，电梯的控制手杖可以在实验室重新制作。
  - English: The elevator can be activated with two parts of the control rod. According to the local cogitator, it can be rebuilt in the laboratory.

#### 9. 杀死费雷克

##### 标题

杀死费雷克

Kill Felek

##### 描述

导航者费雷克·奥赛罗，这座星站的守护者之一，原来是个叛徒。他正是欧拉克五号星站这场暴乱的根源，是时候让这个叛徒为他的谎言与恶行付出代价了。

Felek Orsellio, Navigator and one of the Keepers of the Station, turned out to be a traitor and the source of all the trouble on Eurac V. It is time to punish the traitor for his lies and wickedness.

#### 10. 离开星站

##### 标题

离开星站

Leave the station

##### 描述

卡西娅女士目前是整座星站上唯一幸存的导航者。行商浪人必须立刻把她带回虚空舰，提供必要的医疗援助，为亚空间跳跃仪式做好准备。

Lady Cassia is the only surviving Navigator on the station. She must be immediately brought aboard the Rogue Trader's voidship, provided with the necessary medical aid, and prepared for the communion ritual.

##### 目的地

冯·瓦兰修斯虚空舰，舰桥

Bridge, von Valancius Voidship

### 剧情对话

#### 场景：一个苍白的身影出现在你面前，四肢修长得异乎寻常


- 对话块
  - `Cue_0001`
    - 中文：一个苍白的身影出现在你面前，四肢修长得异乎寻常。她正高举着畸形的双手，上面长着利爪般的指甲。她的双眼仿佛笼罩在血色的迷雾中，鲜血不断地从双眼中流，流满了她如同死人般的苍白面孔。长着刺的腮部隐藏在她凌乱的头发下面。当你接近时，她的腮部紧张地抽动着。
    - English: The pale figure with unnaturally long limbs covers her face with her hands, which are deformed with talon-like nails. Her deathly pale face is coated with blood that continually streams from her scarlet-misted eyes. Her spiny gills, slightly hidden under her dishevelled hair, twitch nervously at your approach.
  - `Cue_0002`
    - 中文：随即，你注意到，这位年轻女子额头上的第三只眼睛隐藏在镶有珠宝的装饰品下面。当你们二人目光相交时，你感觉到了压倒性的力量，足以扼杀灵魂。
    - English: Only now do you notice the third eye on the young woman's forehead, hidden by a jewelled ornament. And when your eyes meet, you sense overwhelming, soul-smothering power.
  - `Cue_49`
    - 中文：当这只古怪的生物目光掠过你时，你的整个心脏都在恐惧中颤抖不止。亚空间给你留下的噩梦，从你记忆的阴影中再次浮现……麻痹了你的意志。
    - English: As the otherworldly creature's gaze slides over you, your entire core shudders in terror. Flashes of past warp nightmares reemerge from the shadows of your memory... and paralyse your will.
  - `Cue_4`
    - 中文：你惊恐地喘着粗气，仿佛被痛苦的巨浪所吞没。你感觉无法呼吸……灼热的眼泪在你的脸上灼烧。为什么会发生这种事情？为什么这种事情会发生在你身上？为什么你感到如此孤独、如此痛苦？这些真的是你的感觉吗？
    - English: You gasp for air in terror, drowning under a crashing wave of pain, you cannot catch your breath... Hot tears burn on your cheeks. Why is this happening? Why is it happening to you? Why do you feel so lonely and in so much pain? Do these feelings even belong to you?

          - English: Argenta is painfully slow in reaching for her weapon, and the next moment her head drops to her chest. /  "I cannot... I cannot!" / The face of the Sister of Battle twists in anger, but her cheeks are glistening with tears.

      - 对话块
        - `Cue_41`
          - 中文：海因里希绷紧了下巴上的肌肉，显然在努力保持着克制态度。 / “‘这玩意儿’是导航宗族的成员，是变种人之中的尊贵成员，负责引导人类虚空舰穿过邪恶的亚空间。好了，行商浪人，别再问愚蠢的问题了，去和你的新任导航者谈判吧。”
          - English: The muscles in Heinrix's jaw twitch as he struggles to maintain self-control. /  "'This' is one of the Navis Nobilite, the noble caste of mutants who guide Humanity's voidships through the treacherous warp. And now, Rogue Trader, stop asking stupid questions and go negotiate with your new Navigator."
  - 选择 `Answer_8`
    - 中文：[克服排山倒海般的绝望感]“我知道我为什么要来这里……所以我会坚定不移地克服所有幻觉！”
    - English: [Overcome the crushing despair] "I know why I am here... and so I will stand strong against any illusion!"
    - 后续
      - 对话块
        - `Cue_12`
          - 中文：你将所有注意力都集中在你的内心。你的心被其他人的痛苦束缚着。在你灼热的内视之下，绝望与痛苦开始减轻。你灵魂中的黑暗渐渐消散，肿痛的喉咙也渐渐地恢复了知觉。你发现你站在某个古怪的生物面前，那是位年轻的女性。当你慢慢地止住眼泪时，她脸上的泪水似乎也不再流淌了。
          - English: You direct all your attention inward — to your heart, currently shackled by another's suffering. Under the gaze of your burning inner eye, the despair and pain begin to dwindle. The darkness in your soul dissipates, the lump in your throat shrinks — and you discover that you are standing in front of a bizarre creature, a young woman whose tears you seem to have dried along with your own.
        - `Cue_0008`
          - 中文：她疲惫地摇了摇头，发出了类似抽泣与受伤的小动物哀鸣的声音。 / 这是……怎么回事？刚刚是有谁在呼唤我的名字吗？所有的叛徒……都已经死了吗？还有你……你是什么人？”
          - English: She wearily shakes her head and lets out a drawn-out sound similar to both a sob and the howl of a small wounded animal. /  "What... is happening? Was someone calling my name? Are all the betrayers... dead already? And you... who are you?"

                - English: Unease settles over her features and she nods cautiously. /  "Pardon my manners, . I did not expect to make such a gracious acquaintance in such a time of great sorrow for our House."

              - `Cue_42`

                - English: Heinrix jerks abruptly as if he intends to dash forward, but someone else is quicker.
              - `Cue_9`
                - 中文：一直跪在附近的老人突然爆发出了低沉的啜泣声。他哭肿的双眼拼命在房间里扫视着，仿佛从刚刚的恍惚中突然清醒了过来。 / “圣子……卡西娅女士，你在哪里？圣子？愿黄金王座保佑——” / 尽管这位导航者年事已高，但他还是一个箭步跳了起来，冲到了年轻女子身边。
                - English: The heavyset old man, who has been kneeling nearby, erupts into low sobs. His eyes, swollen from crying, dart desperately around the room, as though the veil of ignorance has just been ripped away from them. /  "The Child... Lady Cassia, where are you? Sacred Child? Throne preserve—" / Despite his venerable age, the Navigator leaps up and rushes to the young woman's side.
              - `Cue_0029`
                - 中文：“你……” / 老人转过了身子，露出了他的脸。他的脸上布满了漆黑的血管，乳白色的眼睛高高鼓起，仿佛死鱼的眼睛。一股病态的甜味涌进了你的鼻孔里，仿佛这个老人从内到外都在腐烂一样。
                - English: "You..." / The old man shifts, revealing his face to you — it is threaded with jet-black veins, and his bulging, milky eyes bear a striking resemblance to those of a dead fish. A sickly sweet scent assaults your nostrils, as if the old man's flesh is rotting inside his decaying husk.
              - `Cue_0014`
                - 中文：“你竟敢伤害手无寸铁的圣子？竟敢伤害奥赛罗家族的子嗣？无论你是谁，你都要为这样的行为付出鲜血的代价！受死吧！”
                - English: "How dare you injure the defenceless Child, the scion of House Orsellio? Whoever you are, you will pay for this transgression with blood. Prepare to die!"
              - `Cue_0015`
                - 中文：“我的眼睛辜负了我，因为它们无法让我辨别你究竟是敌人还是盟友。我要警告你，一旦你做出了错误的举动，就会招致奥赛罗家族的怒火！”
                - English: "My eyes fail me, for they are unable to make you out as either enemy or ally. I'm warning you, one wrong move will bring the wrath of House Orsellio down upon your head!"
            - 选项组 `Cue_0015`
              - 选择 `Answer_0017`

                - English: "Wait! How can a blind man see the starry sky?"

                      - 中文：作为回应，这个仿佛长着鱼眼睛的导航者目不转睛地盯着你。 / “如果想感知帝皇的光芒，必须要用心去看。黄金王座在上，我的求救信号终于还是传到了小莱卡德！不过，你……你并不是温特斯凯尔王朝的人。”
                      - English: The fish-eyed Navigator goggles at you in response. /  "To perceive the Emperor's light, one must look with the heart. By all the gold on the Throne, my distress signal reached Rykad Minoris after all! But you... you are not from the Winterscale dynasty."

                            - English: Bushy brows furrow in displeasure. /  "Access to the station is no mere privilege — Evayne Winterscale broke the vow of silence he took before House Orsellio! The God-Emperor will judge him. But what about you? Who are you and why have you broken the isolation of Eurac V?"
                    - 选择 `Answer_0029`

                            - 中文：“当涉及到生死时，每个字都至关重要。” / 年迈的导航者关切地看了卡西娅一眼，她此刻不省人事，仿佛死了一样。

Or I will unleash all the horrors of the Sea of Souls upon you! Emperor be my witness!"

                    - English: After the current round of question set `Cue_9` concludes, the dialogue continues into the following content.
                  - 对话块
                    - `Cue_0075`
                      - 中文：帕斯卡的音阵装置发出了二进制颤音。 / “这台神圣机器的机魂需要进行特殊的净化仪式，才能恢复为帝国公民更加熟悉的语言。请求允许访问该装置。”
                      - English: Pasqal's vox-systems emit a binharic trill. /  "The spirits of this sacred machine require special purification rituals in order to restore utilisation of the lingua more familiar to the citizens of the Imperium. Requesting access to the device."
                  - 对话块
                    - `Cue_0002`
                      - 中文：破碎的屏幕上闪烁着跳动的静电。 / “警告！数据损坏。正在处理……正在处理……正在处理……错误，需要手动配置。”
                      - English: The broken screen flickers with dancing static: /  "WARNING! Data corrupted. Processing... Processing... Processing... ERROR. Manual configuration is required."
              - 选择 `Answer_0050`
                - 中文：[返回命令列表]
                - English: [Return to the list of the available commands]
                - 后续
                  - 对话块

                      - English: The vid-screen blinks and the mechanisms in the machine's core emit a quiet hum.
        - 选择 `Answer_0010`
          - 中文：[主电梯控制系统］
          - English: [Main elevator controls]
          - 注：显示条件(Or)：CueSeen；EtudeStatus

            - 选项组 `Cue_0014`
              - 选择 `Answer_0002`

- 对话块
  - `Cue_4`
    - 中文：技术神甫的音阵系统发出了二进制颤音，他的机械触须愤怒地在空气中挥舞着。 / “我在此记录亵渎神明的行为！对高贵的机器犯下如此残忍罪行的人，必须被立刻处决。”
    - English: The Tech-Priest's vox-systems emit a binharic trill, and his mechadendrites start furiously lashing at the air: /  "I am recording blasphemy! The person found guilty of such cruelty to a noble mechanism must be sentenced to immediate destruction."
